[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDuring a fuzzing run of the `fuzz_encode_stream` target in the xz codebase, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer detected a heap-use-after-free error in the function [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`compute_tree_checksum` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `src/xz/src/liblzma/check/treeck.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. A buffer [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated by `create_tree` is freed and then subsequently accessed, leading to an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read from already freed heap memory.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The crash log identifies a heap-use-after-free [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUAF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability. [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer reports reading from an address that was freed earlier in the same[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall sequence.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What Happened  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness `fuzz_encode_stream` invokes `lzma_code` → `stream_encode` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m→ `block_encode` → `lzma_check_update` → `lzma_tree` → `compute_tree_checksum`.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Inside `compute_tree_checksum`, a data structure is allocated by [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`create_tree`.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Later in the same function, that structure is freed [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Despite the free, the code continues and performs an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read from the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed memory region, triggering UAF.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The read is flagged at line [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m in `treeck.c` within `compute_tree_checksum`.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The same function is responsible both for allocating [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `malloc` in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`create_tree`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and freeing the tree buffer, and then erroneously using it after [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfree.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer report shows the allocation stack, the free stack, and the UAF [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccess stack, all confined to `compute_tree_checksum` and its callers.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The issue surfaces under libFuzzer with an interactive fuzzing schedule but is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindependent of the harness beyond providing input to `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Impacted Code Areas  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To understand the full context of this UAF and to verify whether adjacent logic [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis affected, the following files and functions should be reviewed:  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/xz/src/liblzma/check/treeck.c`  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `compute_tree_checksum` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mallocation, free, and checksum logic[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz_encode_stream -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue arises from an AddressSanitizer report during fuzz testing of [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fuzz_encode_stream`. A heap-use-after-free is detected in [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `src/liblzma/check/treeck.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when it frees a tree [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnode and its edges prematurely and later attempts to read from that already-freed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA patch attempt was made by commenting out the two `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls in [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`—one freeing `node->edges` and one freeing `node`—to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent the use-after-free. After applying this patch, the AddressSanitizer error [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisappears but LeakSanitizer reports a large number of direct and indirect memory [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleaks in allocations coming from `[0m[1;35mcreate_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39malso in `treeck.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During execution of `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mfuzz_encode_stream[0m[39m` under libFuzzer with [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer enabled, a heap-use-after-free is reported.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The invalid read occurs at `[0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` line [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m in `treeck.c`. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe function first frees `node->edges` and `node`, then returns `sum`. Due to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecursive calls, freed memory is accessed later in the recursion.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stack trace highlights:  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `[0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mlzma_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mlzma_check_update[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mblock_encode[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mstream_encode[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mlzma_code[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → fuzz harness.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ASan shadow bytes confirm the region had been freed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmarked `fd`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `treeck.c`, the two `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls inside `[0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` were [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommented out:  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```diff[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode->edges[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     + [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode->edges[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     + [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The intent was to eliminate the premature deallocation and thus prevent the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse-after-free.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Result  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After rebuilding with the commented-out frees, AddressSanitizer no longer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreports UAF.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - However, LeakSanitizer now reports:  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A direct leak of [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m bytes from a single object allocated in `[0m[1;35mcreate_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Numerous indirect leaks totaling several kilobytes, all originating from [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecursive calls to `[0m[1;35mcreate_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Every node and its edges allocated by `[0m[1;35mcreate_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remain unfreed.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The lifecycle of tree nodes and edge arrays allocated in `[0m[1;35mcreate_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m33[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m58[0m[39m of `treeck.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: where and when these should be freed.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The role of `[0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in both computing checksums and freeing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory—whether a separate tree destruction function exists or should be introduced.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How `[0m[1;35mlzma_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mlzma_check_update[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` manage the memory allocated for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir checksums and whether they call any cleanup routines.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The interaction between recursive checksum computation and memory deallocation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto ensure no use-after-free and no memory leaks.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
